- **Aesthetic Arc Phase II Batch 0 — Shadcn Default Aliasing (complete):** Micro-session between Phase II audit and Batch 1 implementation. **One file touched, ~50 lines modified in `frontend/src/index.css`.** Every shadcn semantic token in the `:root` + `.dark` blocks aliased to a DESIGN_LANGUAGE equivalent via `var(...)` references. **Platform-wide effect without touching any component code**: 2,886 `text-muted-foreground` usages + 361 `bg-muted` + 163 `bg-background` + 35 `bg-card` + 142 `text-foreground` + 9 `bg-popover` = **3,596 shadcn-default surface/text consumers now render in DL warm-family palette in both modes**. Plus all `bg-primary` / `text-primary` / `border-primary` / `from-primary` / `bg-primary/N` / `ring-ring` / `bg-destructive` / `text-destructive` / `bg-accent` / `bg-secondary` / `bg-sidebar-*` usages now route through DL brass / status-error / brass-subtle / surface-elevated / surface-sunken respectively. **Aliasing preserved (NOT aliased):** `--radius` (shadcn radius scale), `--chart-*` (no DL chart palette yet), `--brand-*` (legacy custom teal), `--status-*-{light,dark}` (coexistence window hex values), **`--ring`** (WCAG concern — brass solid at lightness 0.66 on cream surface is ~2.1:1, FAILS WCAG 2.4.7 3:1 focus-indicator threshold. Shadcn `ring-ring` fallback stays at `oklch(0.48 0 0)` neutral dark gray which passes 4.26:1 against cream. The `.focus-ring-brass` utility remains the brass-ring opt-in; a separate Session 6 cleanup may address its light-mode alpha). **Post-Batch-0 verification on user-reported broken pages:** (a) **MFG dashboard onboarding banner** (line 357-391 `border-primary/20 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary/5 to-primary/10 ... bg-primary/10 ... text-primary`) now renders with brass gradient/border/text automatically — the user's "setup banner" / "emoji rocket" concern resolved by aliasing alone. (b) All `text-muted-foreground` usages across dashboards + scheduling-board family now resolve to warm `content-muted`. (c) **Still broken — require Batch 1 migration**: status pill color maps using `bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800` pattern (MFG line 93-97), widget icon backgrounds using `bg-{color}-50` pattern (MFG 425/432/439/448, FH 126-166), scheduling-board `bg-white` + `bg-slate-50/50` + hardcoded amber/indigo/slate pills, kanban-panel "Failed to load schedule" error card (`bg-white` + `text-red-600`), `bg-white` card chrome throughout kanban/ancillary/direct-ship panels, emoji service-location icons. **Pre-existing latent issue surfaced during audit** (flagged, not fixed): `--ring` keeping current neutral gray doesn't help components using `.focus-ring-brass` utility which fails ~1.26:1 in light mode at 40% alpha on cream surface. Separate cleanup. **Verification:** tsc clean (clean-cache verified), vitest 165/165 unchanged, vite build clean 5.24s. No backend changes. No component code changes. One-file commit. **Mirror discipline maintained** — no DL token values changed, only shadcn aliases added. DESIGN_LANGUAGE.md §3 unchanged.

- **Aesthetic Arc Session 4 — Dark Mode Pass (complete):** Dark mode verification session against DESIGN_LANGUAGE §2 cocktail-lounge-evening mood + WCAG 2.2 AA contrast thresholds. No new components, no net-new aesthetic, no component API changes. Surgical token value adjustments + targeted fixes for Sessions 1-3 misses + one tenant-facing preview feature. **Token surface (tokens.css + DESIGN_LANGUAGE.md §3):** (1) **M1 — dark-mode `status-*-muted` backgrounds tightened** from L 0.28/0.30 → 0.22/0.24, chroma eased proportionally (0.08→0.07 / 0.07→0.06 / 0.06→0.05 / 0.05→0.04). Pre-Session-4 status-text-on-muted-bg was **3.83–4.32:1 (FAIL AA body text)**; post-adjustment **5.0–5.4:1 (PASS)**. Every status-rendering surface (Alert, StatusPill, InlineError, Badge status variants, agent-alerts-card, peek StatusBadge) inherits the fix via semantic token cascade — **zero component code changes**. (2) **m2 — new `--focus-ring-alpha` composable token** (light default 0.40 per DL §6 spec; dark override 0.48) lifts brass focus ring contrast on `--surface-raised` from ~3.00:1 (WCAG 2.4.7 edge) to ~3.5:1. `.focus-ring-brass` utility in `base.css` composes via `color-mix(... calc(var(--focus-ring-alpha) * 100%), transparent)` with 0.40 fallback. **Component fixes:** **M2** — 6 substitutions of `var(--portal-brand-fg, white)` → `var(--portal-brand-fg, var(--content-on-brass))` across `PortalLayout`, `PortalLogin`, `PortalResetPassword`. Fallback is now mode-aware; dark-mode brass-backed text renders as dark charcoal per DL §3 "brass button reads as 'glowing pill with dark text.'" **M5** — `NotificationDropdown` status icons migrated from 4 hardcoded Tailwind primaries (`text-green-500` / `-yellow-500` / `-red-500` / `-blue-500`) to DESIGN_LANGUAGE warm palette (`text-status-{success,warning,error,info}`). Session 3 miss — icons now consistent with Alert/StatusPill/InlineError/Sonner. **m3** — `PortalLayout` logout button focus ring migrated from `focus:ring-white/50` to `focus-visible:ring-[color:var(--portal-brand-fg,var(--content-on-brass))]/50` — mode-aware + scoped to the brand-colored header. **New feature — M3 branding-editor preview:** `/settings/portal-branding` preview panel gains (a) a Light/Dark toggle that scopes `data-mode="dark"` to the preview subtree only (doesn't affect the rest of the admin page the user is currently on), (b) simulated portal page backdrop behind the branded header so admins see how their brand color reads against both cream and dark charcoal, (c) two WCAG contrast readouts — "Brand → header text" with pass/fail against 4.5:1 AA and "Brand against {light|dark} page" with visible/low-contrast advisory (1.5:1 threshold). Proper WCAG sRGB-gamma luminance computed in-component (`_wcagContrast` + `_wcagLuminance`). Closes "tenants save a brand color without seeing dark-mode rendering" audit finding. **Deferred (m1, m4, pre-S3 pages):** `focus-ring-brass` utility gap-ring color uses `--surface-base` per DL §6 spec; on elevated dark surfaces this reads as a subtle darker-than-parent cut (spec-vs-pragmatism call deferred to Session 6). `OfflineBanner` hardcoded `bg-amber-500 text-amber-950` (low priority, transient, mode-identical amber — defer to natural refactor). ~20 pre-Session-3 pages (vault-mold-settings, tax-settings, etc.) remain on long-tail natural-refactor list (documented Session 3). **Tenant brand color approach confirmed Option A** (identical hex in both modes, tenant responsibility) + M3 preview helper as the verification tool. Options B (auto-adjust luminance) and C (separate light/dark colors) explicitly rejected — revisit if production signal shows tenants regularly pick poor-contrast brands. **Mirror discipline canonicalized** in CLAUDE.md §Design System + DESIGN_LANGUAGE.md §3: tokens.css and DL §3 must stay synchronized in the same commit; drift is a defect. **Luminance formula divergence noted as known minor item:** `PortalBrandProvider.applyBrandColor` uses BT.601 luminance; branding-editor preview uses proper WCAG sRGB-gamma luminance; they diverge <5% for most colors. Aligning PortalBrandProvider deferred — see `SPACES_ARCHITECTURE.md §10.6`. **Verification posture:** visual toggles via `data-mode="dark"` on devtools + code-path review + oklch-lightness → sRGB-linear-Y contrast calculations. **WCAG compliance (post-Session-4, dark mode):** text-on-surface AAA across all levels; status-text-on-muted AA (5.0–5.4:1); brass-text-on-brass AAA (6.4:1); focus rings pass 3:1 across all surfaces (~3.5:1 minimum on raised). **No new tests shipped** — token value changes aren't testable via unit tests and vitest component tests don't reference specific color values. Baseline vitest 165/165 unchanged, tsc clean, build clean. **Arc status:** 4/6 sessions complete. Next: Session 5 (motion pass), then Session 6 (final QA).

- **Workflow Arc Phase 8e.2.1 — Portal Completion (complete):** Closes every item 8e.2 deferred to §10.11. Tenant admins now manage portal users + branding from `/settings/*`; the 4 remaining driver pages mount under `/portal/<slug>/driver/*`; reset-password lives at `/portal/<slug>/reset-password`. **The James dogfood flow works end-to-end on first invocation** — invite → branded email → reset password → log in → see today's route → mark a stop delivered → submit mileage. **Migration `r44_drivers_employee_id_nullable`**: relaxes the NOT NULL on `drivers.employee_id` so portal-created Drivers (no tenant `User` link) can exist; logs before-row-counts at upgrade time for operator visibility. **Actual column drop deferred** to a latent-bug cleanup session because removing the column before production data has drifted through the full migration window risks a tricky rollback. Guarding test `test_employee_id_is_nullable_after_r44` keeps the invariant. **Migration `r45_portal_invite_email_template`**: D-7 managed template `email.portal_invite` seeded idempotently — subject "Welcome to the {{ tenant_name }} driver portal", onboarding body distinct from the existing `email.portal_password_recovery`. **New admin router** `app/api/routes/portal_admin.py` mounted at `/api/v1/portal/admin/*`. Registered BEFORE `portal.router` in `api/v1.py` so the public `@router.get("/{tenant_slug}/branding")` doesn't swallow `/portal/admin/branding` by matching `tenant_slug="admin"` — test caught it immediately, explanatory comment prevents regression. Thirteen endpoints: list/invite/edit/deactivate/reactivate/unlock/reset-password/resend-invite for users + GET/PATCH branding + POST /branding/logo. **Logo upload hardening**: PNG/JPG only (SVG explicitly rejected for embedded-script safety), ≤2 MB, 50–1024 px dimensions, Pillow-verified (`img.verify()` + reopen for `.size`). Stored at stable R2 key `tenants/{company_id}/portal/logo.{ext}` via `legacy_r2_client.upload_bytes`; updates `Company.logo_url`. **Service layer additions** in `app/services/portal/user_service.py`: 7 new admin CRUD functions (`list_portal_users_for_tenant` / `update_portal_user_profile` / `deactivate_portal_user` / `reactivate_portal_user` / `unlock_portal_user` / `issue_admin_reset_password` / `resend_invite`) + `PortalUserSummary` frozen dataclass (derives `status` from is_active/locked_until/hashed_password + resolves `assigned_space_name` from tenant-admin preferences + joins to active Driver for `driver_id`). **Auto-create Driver row on invite** — `_is_driver_space_template` predicate checks admin user's `preferences.spaces` JSONB for a space with `name == "Driver"` (case-insensitive, exact match). Only that triggers `_maybe_auto_create_driver_row`, which inserts `Driver(employee_id=None, portal_user_id=new_pu.id, active=True)` idempotently. Future yard-operator/removal-staff/family/supplier portals will NOT accidentally become drivers — predicate is deliberately narrow. **5 new portal driver-data mirror endpoints** at `/portal/drivers/me/{route,stops/{id},stops/{id}/exception,stops/{id}/status,mileage}`. Each follows the canonical thin-router-over-service pattern (SPACES_ARCHITECTURE.md §10.7): resolve `portal_user → Driver via portal_user_id` via `resolve_driver_for_portal_user`, then delegate to `driver_mobile_service`. **Zero duplication** of route-loading or stop-status logic. Driver-scoped isolation: cross-driver stop access 404s; tenant context comes from the portal JWT (no `X-Company-Slug` header dependency on portal-authed endpoints). **Dual-identity migration for Driver**: legacy `employee_id` path preserved for reading existing data; new drivers use the canonical `portal_user_id` path. `delivery_service.get_driver_by_employee` → deprecation stub with `DeprecationWarning`. `deliveries.py::list_drivers` enriches display names from both paths. `widget_data.team_driver_performance` rewritten from INNER JOIN on `employee_id` to a LEFT JOIN over both identity paths — widget now shows every active driver regardless of which identity path they arrived through. **Legacy `POST /api/v1/delivery/drivers` retired** — explanatory comment in `deliveries.py` + frontend `delivery-service.createDriver` throws an error pointing to `/settings/portal-users`. Manual `Driver` inserts still permitted for migrations and tests; the HTTP-addressable create endpoint is gone. **Frontend admin UI**: `/settings/portal-users` (~400 LOC, Session 3 primitives — Table + StatusPill + DropdownMenu + Dialog, status filter, per-row action menu, Invite dialog filters space options to portal spaces only) + `/settings/portal-branding` (~300 LOC, logo upload with client-side preview + 8 color swatches + hex input + live preview pane that temporarily applies `--portal-brand` CSS var on mount/unmount). **4 portal driver pages + reset-password page** (~700 LOC total): `PortalDriverRoute` (mobile-first stop list with 88 px touch targets, StatusPill per stop, Log mileage CTA, offline error handling), `PortalStopDetail` (address/contacts, 3 h-12 action buttons Mark delivered/arrived/Report exception, exception dialog with Select + Textarea, Google Maps deep link, offline toasts), `PortalMileage` (start/end mileage `type="number" inputMode="decimal"` font-plex-mono digits, live delta display, end≥start validation), `PortalResetPassword` (token-gated, 8-char min + confirmation, success navigates to login). **`OfflineBanner` mounted inside `PortalLayout`** (not top-level `PortalApp`) — only renders in the authed shell. **`PortalApp` route tree extended** with 4 new routes (reset-password outside the auth guard since the link arrives pre-session). **Frontend tsc clean**, vitest 165/165 (unchanged — no vitest-tier tests for portal admin yet; pytest + Playwright cover the critical paths). **Tests shipped Phase 8e.2.1**: 31 new in `backend/tests/test_portal_phase8e21.py` across 8 test classes (admin list + invite × 5, auto-create Driver × 2, admin lifecycle × 5, branding admin × 3, logo upload validation × 6, legacy retirement × 1, portal driver data mirror × 8, admin routes cross-realm × 1) + 7 Playwright mobile scenarios in `portal-phase-8e21.spec.ts` (driver route list, stop detail mark-delivered, mileage validation, reset-password branded token param, reset-password missing token, 44 px touch-target audit on stop detail, OfflineBanner offline event). **Full portal regression (8e.2 + 8e.2.1): 58/58 passing, no regressions.** **Deferred to post-8e.2.1**: actual column drop on `drivers.employee_id`, `invite`↔`recovery` token column consolidation (they share `recovery_token` today), full mobile touch-target lint on every portal interactive element, vehicle inspection page, tenant-logo SVG support with server-side sanitization. **Arc sequencing**: 8e.2.1 complete → Aesthetic 4–5 → 8f → 8g → Aesthetic 6 → cleanup → 8h finale.

FH driver still has no template (FH removal staff dispatches through case workflows). **Phase 8e.2 defers to 8e.2.1**: tenant admin UI for portal user management, branding editor UI, remaining 4 driver pages mounted under portal routes, offline-tolerance touches, full mobile polish, reset-password page. **Tests shipped Phase 8e.2**: 25 new in `test_portal_phase8e2.py` across 9 test classes (schema × 4, auth service × 4, password recovery × 2, cross-realm isolation × 4 LOAD-BEARING, branding × 2, login endpoint × 3, SpaceConfig modifiers × 2, MFG driver template × 1, driver data mirror × 2, non-destructive migration × 1) + 3 Playwright smoke tests (branded login, driver home post-login, no DotNav/cmdbar/settings). **Full Phase 1–8e.2 regression: 379 backend tests passing, no regressions.** Frontend vitest 165/165, tsc 0 errors, build clean 6.36s. **Arc sequencing**: 8e.2.1 (portal admin UI + branding editor + driver pages polish) → Aesthetic 4-5 → 8f → 8g → Aesthetic 6 → cleanup → 8h finale. **Ships before September Wilbert demo.**

- **Workflow Arc Phase 8e.1 — Smart Spaces (complete):** Topical affinity layer on top of Phase 8e's spaces fabric + full `/settings/spaces` customization page + command bar integrations beyond Phase 3's pin boost. **Users don't configure "what this space is about" — the system infers it from behavior.** Signal is implicit, computation automatic, result is a command bar that responds to the user's actual workflow. **New `user_space_affinity` table** (migration `r41_user_space_affinity`): composite PK on `(user_id, space_id, target_type, target_id)`, CHECK constraint on 4-value target_type enum, two partial indexes (`ix_user_space_affinity_user_space_active` for the read prefetch + `ix_user_space_affinity_user_recent_active` for future-proofing). Storage bounded by `pins × spaces` per user (~140 rows steady-state). **`app/services/spaces/affinity.py`**: `record_visit` (PostgreSQL UPSERT via `ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE`), `prefetch_for_user_space` (one indexed query per command_bar query → in-memory dict), `boost_factor` (pure formula `1.0 + 0.4 * log10(visit+1)/log10(11) * max(0, 1-age_days/30)` — saturates at 10 visits → 1.40×, decays over 30 days), `delete_affinity_for_space` (cascade helper), `clear_affinity_for_user` (GDPR), `count_for_user` (counter). In-memory 60s throttle bucket keyed on `(user_id, target_type, target_id)` — defense-in-depth over client throttle. **3 new API endpoints**: `POST /api/v1/spaces/affinity/visit` (fire-and-forget, returns `{recorded:bool}` — 200 even when throttled, 400 invalid target_type, 404 unknown space_id), `GET /api/v1/spaces/affinity/count?space_id=...` (`{count:int}`), `DELETE /api/v1/spaces/affinity?space_id=...` (`{cleared:int}`, idempotent). **Route ordering invariant**: `/affinity/*` routes declared BEFORE `/{space_id}` routes — otherwise FastAPI would match `DELETE /affinity` against `DELETE /{space_id}` with `space_id="affinity"`. Cascade on space delete: `crud.delete_space` removes affinity rows in the same transaction. **Command bar retrieval integration** (`retrieval.py`): three multiplicative boosts — Phase 3 pin (1.25×, unchanged) + Phase 8e.1 starter-template (1.10× for results matching role-template pins even if unpinned, skipped when pin boost applied — not additive) + Phase 8e.1 affinity (1.0–1.40× per formula). Max compound stack pinned+affinity'd+today = 1.75× (above the 1.5 single-boost ceiling; acceptable for heavily-used pinned targets). New helpers: `_active_space_starter_template_targets(user, active_space_id)` + `_affinity_factor_for_result(item, affinity, boost_for_target)`. **Frontend affinity layer**: types + service methods (`recordAffinityVisit` fire-and-forget, `getAffinityCount`, `clearAffinityHistory`), `useAffinityVisit` hook (module-scoped throttle Map, 60s window matches server), `AffinityVisitWatcher` component mounted at app root under `SpaceProvider` (watches `useLocation().pathname`, matches starts-with for nav_item / exact for saved_view + triage_queue against active-space pins). **4 write trigger surfaces wired**: PinnedSection pin click (onNavigate callback on Link), PinStar ONLY on pin-TO-pinned transition (unpinning is not intent), CommandBar navigate branch (target_type inferred from action.type + route, with prefix-stripping for backend `entity:<type>:<uuid>` / `saved_view:<uuid>` shapes), AffinityVisitWatcher URL-match. Five anti-triggers explicitly excluded (DotNav space switch, keyboard cycling, unpin, hover peek, non-activated result). **`/settings/spaces` customization page** (~900 LOC) built strictly on Aesthetic Arc Session 3 primitives (Alert, StatusPill, Tooltip, Popover, FormSection, FormStack, Card, Dialog, brass focus): 2-column layout (sidebar + main editor), drag-reorder user spaces (system spaces sticky leftmost), full space editing (name, icon via 16-entry Popover picker, 6-accent picker with hover-live-preview via temporary `--space-accent` CSS var, density, is_default, landing-route dropdown sourced from pins + /dashboard + preserved custom), pin manager with drag-reorder + per-pin "Move to…" Popover for transferring pins between spaces, reapply-defaults action with confirmation-before-commit modal explicitly clarifying "won't change customizations" per user spec, type-to-confirm `Reset spaces` destructive modal, template picker dialog, affinity counter card ("N tracked signals") with "Clear learning history" action, `welcome_to_settings_spaces` onboarding touch. **Dialog deep-links**: `NewSpaceDialog` gains "More options…" footer link to `/settings/spaces?new=1`; `SpaceEditorDialog` gains "Manage all pins, move items between spaces, import templates…" link to `/settings/spaces#pins-<space_id>`. Both dialogs remain DotNav quick-path; `/settings/spaces` is the power surface. Coexist strategy. **Purpose-limitation clause** documented in `SPACES_ARCHITECTURE.md` §9.4: affinity data used ONLY for command bar ranking; future use (briefings recommendations, dashboard personalization, saved-view recommendations) requires separate scope-expansion audit. Load-bearing for user trust. **Performance (BLOCKING gate preserved)**: command_bar_query baseline pre-8e.1 p50=7.9ms/p99=10.3ms; post-8e.1 with affinity rows seeded p50=**8.2ms**/p99=**77.3ms** — 12×/3.9× headroom on 100/300ms budget. `test_command_bar_latency.py` extended to seed 10 affinity rows + active space so the prefetch+boost pipeline is exercised in measurements. **Tests shipped Phase 8e.1**: 33 new in `test_spaces_phase8e1_affinity.py` across 10 test classes (schema/formula/record_visit/prefetch/isolation/cascade/clear/API/starter-template/composition) + BLOCKING latency gate = 34 new. **Full Phase 1–8e.1 spaces regression**: 151 passing, no regressions. **Migration head advances** `r40_aftercare_email_template` → `r41_user_space_affinity`. **Arc sequencing**: 8e.1 complete → 8e.2 (portal foundation with MFG driver reconnaissance) → Aesthetic 4-5 → 8f → 8g → Aesthetic 6 → bug cleanup → 8h finale.

- **Workflow Arc Phase 8e — Spaces and Default Views (complete):** Expands Phase 3 Spaces with template coverage for previously-unmapped office roles, a deliberate-activation landing-route field, two new onboarding touches, and the reapply-defaults escape hatch. **Drivers and other operational roles are explicitly excluded** — they get portal UX in Phase 8e.2, not platform Space templates. **6 new (vertical, role_slug) combinations**: cemetery/admin (Operations + Administrative + Ownership), cemetery/office (Administrative + Operational), crematory/admin (Operations + Administrative), crematory/office (Operations + Administrative), funeral_home/accountant (Books + Reports), manufacturing/accountant (Books + Reports + Compliance). **2 enrichments**: manufacturing/safety_trainer promoted from FALLBACK to dedicated Compliance (with `safety_program_triage` pin) + Training spaces; manufacturing/production Production space gained `safety_program_triage` pin alongside existing `task_triage`. **Template coverage after 8e**: 13 (vertical, role_slug) combinations + 1 system space + 1 fallback (up from 6). **New SpaceConfig.default_home_route field**: deliberate activation (DotNav click, Switch-to-X command-bar result) navigates to the space's landing route; keyboard activation (⌘[, ⌘], ⌘⇧1..7) does not. `SpaceContext.switchSpace(spaceId, { source: "deliberate" | "keyboard" })` contract; default when omitted = `"keyboard"` (safer). All 14 shipped templates carry a route. **Landing-route authoring UI** in SpaceEditorDialog dropdown populated from pins + /dashboard + existing custom value; unavailable pins excluded. **Saved-view seed dependency verification**: 6 new saved-view seed combos added to `saved_views/seed.py` alongside the new space templates; `TestSavedViewSeedDependencies` fails loudly if any space template pin points at a missing seed key. **MAX_SPACES_PER_USER bumped 5 → 7** in lockstep across backend + frontend; DotNav tightened `gap-1.5 → gap-1` + `overflow-x-auto` to fit 7 dots + plus in the 240px sidebar; `Cmd+⇧1..5` → `Cmd+⇧1..7`. **Reapply-defaults endpoint** at `POST /api/v1/spaces/reapply-defaults` wrapping `user_service.reapply_role_defaults_for_user` (idempotent on saved_views + spaces via per-role preferences arrays). **Two new Phase-7-style onboarding touches**: `welcome_to_spaces` on DotNav (≥2 spaces gate); `pin_this_view` on PinStar (unpinned-target gate). Phase 8e.2 is the reconnaissance phase with MFG driver as the first concrete portal; ships before September Wilbert demo. **Tests shipped Phase 8e**: 31 new in `test_spaces_phase8e.py` across 7 test classes (TestPhase8eTemplates × 6 parametrized, TestPhase8eEnrichments × 2, TestNoDriverTemplates × 3 portal-deferral invariant, TestSavedViewSeedDependencies × 3, TestDefaultHomeRoute × 8, TestMaxSpacesBump × 2, TestReapplyDefaultsEndpoint × 3, TestNavLabelCoverage × 1, TestDefaultHomeRouteViaAPI × 3). 2 pre-existing tests updated for the 8e contract: `test_spaces_api.py::test_space_cap_enforced_at_api` (bumped 5 → 7), `test_space_pins_triage_queue.py` × 2 (Production now has 2 triage pins). **Full Phase 1–8e regression: 117 spaces tests passing**, no regressions across saved_views (49) + briefings (16) + command_bar_latency neighbors. **Migration head unchanged** at `r40_aftercare_email_template` — Phase 8e is pure JSONB + service-layer work; no schema change. **Updated arc sequencing**: 8e (ships now) → 8e.1 (smart spaces — topical affinity + `/settings/spaces` customization UI) → 8e.2 (portal foundation with MFG driver reconnaissance) → Aesthetic Sessions 4-5 → 8f remaining accounting migrations → 8g dashboard → Aesthetic 6 QA → bug cleanup → 8h arc finale.

- **Workflow Arc Phase 8d.1 — Safety Program Migration (complete):** Single-migration reconnaissance phase for **AI-generation-with-approval shape** — the most architecturally interesting remaining workflow. `wf_sys_safety_program_gen` migrates from 4 placeholder description steps to a single `call_service_method` → `safety_program.run_generation_pipeline`. **New per-run cardinality** (Template v2.2 §10, sixth): the triage queue reads `SafetyProgramGeneration WHERE status='pending_review'` directly — no AgentJob wrapper, no AgentAnomaly, no new schema column. The status machine (`draft / pending_review / approved / rejected`) predates the arc (r15_safety_program_generation), so Phase 8d.1 is purely a UX alternate — triage queue + bespoke `/safety/programs` UI coexist indefinitely. **AI-generation-content-invariant parity (Template v2.2 §5.5.5)**: the parity test seeds `SafetyProgramGeneration` rows directly with pre-populated `generated_content` + `generated_html`, then runs approval through both `svc.approve_generation` and `safety_program_adapter.approve_generation` — byte-identical field writes on `SafetyProgramGeneration` + `SafetyProgram` are asserted. AI output reproducibility is never tested (Claude is non-deterministic); the parity claim shifts to approval mechanics only. **Scheduler retirement (Template v2.2 §7.7)**: the pre-8d.1 `job_safety_program_generation` APScheduler cron in `backend/app/scheduler.py` is retired with explanatory comments replacing 3 usages (function definition, `JOB_REGISTRY` entry, `add_job` block). The workflow scheduler's `scheduled` dispatch now owns the monthly firing via `wf_sys_safety_program_gen`'s `cron="0 6 1 * *"` + `timezone="America/New_York"` — tenant-local 6am is an improvement over the prior UTC-only APScheduler cron. Double-fire avoided. Unit test `test_job_registry_has_no_safety_program_entry` enforces. **AI panel included** (first migration-arc queue with AI-assisted review of AI-generated artifacts). Prompt `triage.safety_program_context_question` seeded idempotently via `scripts/seed_triage_phase8d1.py` (Option A pattern: created / noop / updated / skipped_custom). Four chips: "How does this program change from last year's?" / "Are there OSHA requirements for {{topic_title}} I should verify are in here?" / "Is this program appropriate for a precast concrete operation?" / "What sections need the most scrutiny for compliance?". System prompt carries explicit **VERTICAL-APPROPRIATE TERMINOLOGY** block (precast concrete / burial vault hazards) + **COMPLIANCE DISCIPLINE** block (hallucination in regulatory citations causes legal exposure; cite the scrape snippet or say "would need to check the full standard at <scrape_url>"). **Related entities builder** returns a 5-entity payload: generation (metadata + token usage), safety_training_topic (title + OSHA code + key_points), osha_scrape (500-char snippet + scrape_url), prior SafetyProgram version (1000-char content_snippet — "what's changing from last year"), generated PDF Document (presigned URL via D-1, 1-hour TTL). **Engraved urn two-gate and other service-only workflows** remain intentionally service-only (documented in Phase 8d). **Zero duplication**: adapter's approve/reject delegate to `svc.approve_generation` / `svc.reject_generation` verbatim — no logic rewritten. **Pre-existing latent bug surfaced** (flagged for separate D-model hygiene session, NOT fixed in 8d.1): `safety_program_generations.pdf_document_id` FK still points at `documents_legacy` (0 rows) instead of canonical `documents` (170 rows) after Phase D-1's rename. Production's `generate_pdf` writes a canonical Document then fails the FK check, silently swallowed by `run_monthly_generation`'s non-fatal try/except — explains why production PDFs don't link back to generations today. Template v2.2 §15 entry #7 catalogs it. **Tests shipped Phase 8d.1**: 13 BLOCKING parity (9 categories: approval-field-identity + version-increment + rejection-field-identity + reject-without-reason + non-pending-review rejection + no-SafetyProgram-on-reject + no-Document-re-render + cross-tenant isolation + pipeline-scale equivalence) + 2 BLOCKING latency gates + 16 unit + 6 Playwright scenarios = **37 new tests**. Full Phase 8a/8b/8c/8d regression: **171 passing, no regressions**. **Actual latency (dev hardware)**: `safety_program_triage` next_item p50=5.7ms / p99=7.6ms (17× / 40× headroom); apply_action p50=10.0ms / p99=13.3ms (20× / 38× headroom). Migration head unchanged (no new DB migration — per-run cardinality reuses existing status column). **Template v2.2** ships alongside the migration with three additions: §5.5.5 AI-generation-content-invariant parity, §7.7 legacy APScheduler cron removal convention, §10 sixth cardinality (per-run) distinct from per-staging-row by the "pre-existing state machine" criterion. **Ready for Aesthetic Arc Session 2 (core component refresh)**.

- **Workflow Arc Phase 8d — Vertical Workflow Migrations (complete):** Two workflow migrations (`wf_fh_aftercare_7day` FH tier-3 + `wf_sys_catalog_fetch` MFG tier-1) plus a corrective data migration fixing an r36 scope-backfill bug that affected 10 workflows. **r38_fix_vertical_scope_backfill** closes the r36 misclassification: r36's backfill used `WHEN tier = 1 THEN 'core'` which ignored the `vertical` column, filing 10 vertical-specific tier-1 workflows under `scope='core'`. The correction sets scope='vertical' for all 10 (legacy_print_proof/final, safety_program_gen, vault_order_fulfillment, document_review_reminder, auto_delivery, catalog_fetch, ss_certificate, scribe_processing, plot_reservation). Regression gate `test_r38_scope_backfill_fix.py` enforces the post-r38 invariant `tier=1 AND vertical IS NOT NULL IMPLIES scope='vertical'`. The Phase 8a companion test was tightened from `test_tier_1_workflows_are_core` to `test_tier_1_cross_vertical_workflows_are_core` (the other half of the symmetric rule). **r39_catalog_publication_state**: new `urn_catalog_sync_logs.publication_state` column (`pending_review / published / rejected / superseded`) + partial index on pending-review; enables triage-gated catalog publishing. Pre-r39 rows backfill to `published` preserving legacy auto-publish semantics. **r40_aftercare_email_template**: seeds `email.fh_aftercare_7day` managed template — closes a silent bug where the pre-8d `wf_fh_aftercare_7day` seed referenced a phantom template_key (`"aftercare_7day"`) that didn't exist anywhere in the D-2 template registry. Aftercare emails would have silently no-op'd if the scheduler fired. **Two new adapters** at `backend/app/services/workflows/`: `aftercare_adapter.py` (triage-only; run_pipeline stages AgentAnomalies per eligible case, approve_send renders template + logs VaultItem, skip_case + request_review resolve anomaly with audit trail) and `catalog_fetch_adapter.py` (triage-gated publish; run_staged_fetch downloads + MD5-diffs + archives to R2 + creates pending-review sync_log, approve_publish fetches R2 bytes + runs legacy `WilbertIngestionService.ingest_from_pdf` unchanged + flips publication_state, reject_publish flips to rejected with reason). **Supersede semantics** on catalog_fetch: a newer fetch marks older pending-review rows as `superseded` so the queue never holds two competing catalogs. **NO AI question panels on 8d queues** per user-approved scope decision — aftercare + catalog_fetch are audit/retry workspaces, not decision workspaces. The invariant is test-enforced at `test_phase8d_unit.py::test_no_ai_question_panels_on_phase8d_queues`. **Engraved urn two-gate documented as intentionally service-only**: the urn_engraving workflow ships a token-based public FH approval URL (`/proof-approval/{token}`, 72-hour expiry, no auth) + staff approval. Migration would invert the customer-facing URL contract for no platform benefit — explicitly retained as service-owned. **Zero duplication discipline**: aftercare emails render from the D-2 managed template via `delivery_service.send_email_with_template`; catalog publication calls `WilbertIngestionService.ingest_from_pdf` unchanged against R2-staged bytes. Both adapters reuse the AgentJob + AgentAnomaly container pattern from Phase 8b/8c. **Safelist + triage extensions**: 2 new `_SERVICE_METHOD_REGISTRY` entries (`aftercare.run_pipeline`, `catalog_fetch.run_staged_fetch`), 2 new `_DIRECT_QUERIES` (`aftercare_triage`, `catalog_fetch_triage`), 6 new HANDLERS (send/skip/request_review + approve/reject/request_review), 2 new platform_default queue configs. `_RELATED_ENTITY_BUILDERS` deliberately NOT extended — only needed when queues carry AI question panels, which 8d doesn't. **Seed rewrites**: `wf_fh_aftercare_7day` collapses 2-step (send_email + log_vault_item referencing phantom template) into 1-step `call_service_method` → `aftercare.run_pipeline`; `wf_sys_catalog_fetch` collapses 2-step (system_job + notify) into 1-step `call_service_method` → `catalog_fetch.run_staged_fetch`. **Deferred to Phase 8d.1**: `wf_sys_safety_program_gen` (Claude Sonnet + WeasyPrint + SafetyProgramGeneration row writes + month-ahead lookahead — deserves its own reconnaissance session; first workflow-arc migration exercising AI-generation-with-approval-gating). **Tests shipped**: 39 new (20 unit + 10 aftercare parity + 10 catalog_fetch parity + 4 BLOCKING latency gates + 3 r38 regression + 6 Playwright scenarios). Phase 8a/8b/8c regression: **140 passing, no regressions**. **Actual latency (dev hardware)**: aftercare_triage next_item p50=30.3ms / apply_action p50=22.1ms (3.3× / 9× headroom); catalog_fetch_triage next_item p50=2.9ms / apply_action p50=5.5ms (34× / 36× headroom). Migration head: `r37_approval_gate_email_template` → `r38_fix_vertical_scope_backfill` → `r39_catalog_publication_state` → `r40_aftercare_email_template`.

- **Polish and Arc Finale — Phase 7 of UI/UX Arc (complete — ARC FINALE):** Phase 7 is the finale of the UI/UX arc. No new primitives, no new feature work — a deliberate pass over every interstitial moment (empty, loading, error, first-run, transition, mobile, accessibility) across the 6 phases shipped before it. 15 sequential polish tasks produced: 3 shared UI primitives (`EmptyState`, `Skeleton`, `InlineError`), 10 per-surface empty state replacements (7 saved view renderers + TasksList + TriagePage caught-up + TriageIndex + CommandBar no-results + SavedViewsIndex + BriefingPage + BriefingCard), 5 skeleton replacements, 1 retry-fetch hook with auto-retry-once (BriefingPage) + Triage action retry that preserves the queue item, a server-side first-run tooltip infrastructure (`User.preferences.onboarding_touches_shown`, cross-device, 5 wired tooltips at command bar / saved view / space switcher / triage / briefing), ARIA labels + aria-live on CommandBar / NLOverlay / TriagePage / BriefingPage, a `?` key context-aware `KeyboardHelpOverlay` mounted at app root, mobile 44px touch-target fixes (triage action palette, flow controls, briefing prefs), `OfflineBanner` + `useOnlineStatus` hook, a global `prefers-reduced-motion` retrofit in `index.css` neutralizing every transition + animation across the 6 prior phases without individual file edits, motion-safe micro-interactions on NL extraction entrance + triage item transitions, WCAG AA contrast verification for all 6 space accents (ALL 6 PASS — zero remediation needed) at `backend/tests/test_arc_accent_contrast.py`, and a focus-ring contrast remediation at `backend/tests/test_arc_focus_ring_contrast.py` + `--ring` darkened from `oklch(0.708 0 0)` to `oklch(0.48 0 0)` in `index.css` so focus indicators pass WCAG 3:1 against white + all 6 accent-light chips. **Telemetry** shipped as a minimal Intelligence-table + in-memory-counter surface at `/bridgeable-admin/telemetry` — platform-admin-gated; shows p50/p99/request-count/error-rate for the 5 arc endpoints (command_bar_query / saved_view_execute / nl_extract / triage_next_item / triage_apply_action) plus Intelligence aggregations over 24h/7d/30d with per-caller-module cost breakdown. Honest expectation-setting: the page explicitly states counters are per-process + clear on restart. `app/services/arc_telemetry.py` provides `record(endpoint, latency_ms, errored)` + `snapshot()`; each of the 5 endpoints wraps its handler in try/finally with the timing record. New backend route `/api/platform/admin/arc-telemetry` reads intelligence_executions aggregates. **Zero new database tables** per approved scope. **Arc documentation finale** (see next three bullets). **Tests**: 8 new contrast + focus-ring tests (all passing), total 288 backend tests across Phase 1-7 regression — no regressions. tsc 0 errors. All 5 BLOCKING latency gates from Phases 1-6 still green. Post-arc backlog documented in `UI_UX_ARC.md` (~45 items across 10 categories). Migration head unchanged at `r35_briefings_table`.

### UI/UX Arc (Phases 1-7) — Complete

Seven-phase arc that rebuilt Bridgeable's user-facing surface as a composable platform. Started April 2026, finished April 2026. Each phase shipped working + tested + documented; no phase was abandoned mid-stream. The arc establishes seven platform primitives + architectural patterns that future features compose rather than duplicate.

**The seven primitives:**
1. **Command bar** (Phase 1) — `POST /api/v1/command-bar/query` platform layer: intent classifier + pg_trgm resolver + registry + retrieval orchestrator. p50=5.0ms/p99=6.9ms. BLOCKING CI gate at 100/300ms.
2. **Saved views** (Phase 2) — storage in `vault_items.metadata_json.saved_view_config`; 7 presentation modes (list, table, kanban, calendar, cards, chart, stat); cross-tenant field masking; visibility levels; seed per role. p50=15.4ms/p99=18.5ms.
3. **Spaces** (Phase 3) — per-user workspace contexts stored in `User.preferences.spaces` (JSONB, no new table); 6 visual accents (all WCAG AA verified in Phase 7); pinned items via server-side pin resolution; `Cmd+[`/`Cmd+]`/`Cmd+Shift+1-5` shortcuts.
4. **Natural Language Creation** (Phase 4) — Fantastical-style live overlay. Pipeline: structured parsers (<5ms) → pg_trgm resolver (<30ms) → Haiku AI fallback. 5 entity types supported (case, event, contact, task, sales_order). p50=5.9ms/p99=7.2ms on no-AI path; ~350ms with Haiku.
5. **Triage Workspace** (Phase 5) — keyboard-driven decision stream. Pluggable 7-component configs (item display, action palette, context panels, embedded actions, flow controls, collaboration, intelligence). 2 shipped queues (task_triage, ss_cert_triage). SS cert parity test asserts triage path produces identical side effects as legacy UI. next_item p50=4.8ms/p99=5.8ms; apply_action p50=9.7ms/p99=13.5ms.
6. **Morning and Evening Briefings** (Phase 6) — AI narrative synthesis over the primitives. First per-user scheduled pattern on platform (every-15-min global sweep + per-user window check). Legacy `briefing_service.py` coexist-not-absorb. Space-aware prompts. p50=28.9ms/p99=32ms.
7. **Polish infrastructure** (Phase 7) — `EmptyState` / `Skeleton` / `InlineError` shared UI primitives + `useRetryableFetch` + `useOnboardingTouch` / `OnboardingTouch` (cross-device) + `KeyboardHelpOverlay` + `OfflineBanner` + `useOnlineStatus` + global `prefers-reduced-motion` retrofit + WCAG contrast verification + minimal telemetry.

**Cross-phase architectural patterns (established by the arc):**
- **In-code platform defaults + vault_item tenant overrides** — used by triage queue configs (Phase 5), saved view seeds (Phase 2), space templates (Phase 3). The pattern: platform-global configs live in Python; tenants override via vault_items that layer on top at read time.
- **Parallel resolver paths** — command bar fires 4 resolvers in parallel (Phase 1-2), NL creation fires structured + resolver + AI in sequence (Phase 4); both compose without blocking the hot path.
- **Registry singletons with side-effect imports** — action registry (Phase 5), triage platform defaults (Phase 5), saved-view entity registry (Phase 2); each imports a `*_defaults.py` at package init to populate the singleton.
- **Role-based seeding with idempotency arrays in `User.preferences`** — `saved_views_seeded_for_roles` (Phase 2), `spaces_seeded_for_roles` (Phase 3), `briefings_seeded_for_roles` (Phase 6), `onboarding_touches_shown` (Phase 7). Same pattern: track what's been seeded per role, skip on re-run.
- **Adapter pattern for registry evolution** — `commandBarQueryAdapter.ts` (Phase 1, interface-only) matured into the Phase 5 `services/actions/` full reshape without breaking backend contract.
- **Coexist-with-legacy over rewrite** — Phase 6 briefings compose the 1,869-line legacy `briefing_service.py` context builders as dependencies rather than rewriting. Phase 5 routes (`/briefings/v2/*`) coexist with legacy `/briefings/briefing`. Post-arc cleanup is deliberate, not mandatory.
- **BLOCKING CI latency gates per primitive** — every phase that shipped an endpoint-hot-path shipped a latency test that fails CI if regressed. 5 gates total across the arc.
- **Honest expectation-setting in admin UIs** — telemetry page documents "counters clear on restart"; scheduler sweep documents "first per-user scheduled pattern" in CLAUDE.md §10 for future features to inherit.

**Performance envelope (production dev-hardware, arc-complete):**

| Endpoint | p50 | p99 | Budget | Headroom p50 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| command_bar_query | 5.0 ms | 6.9 ms | 100 / 300 ms | 20× |
| saved_view_execute | 15.4 ms | 18.5 ms | 150 / 500 ms | 10× |
| nl_extract (no AI) | 5.9 ms | 7.2 ms | 600 / 1200 ms | 100× |
| triage_next_item | 4.8 ms | 5.8 ms | 100 / 300 ms | 20× |
| triage_apply_action | 9.7 ms | 13.5 ms | 200 / 500 ms | 20× |
| briefing_generate | 28.9 ms | 32.0 ms | 2000 / 5000 ms | 69× |

**Total across the arc**: 7 migrations (r29 notification_safety_merge through r35_briefings_table); 6 new tables (triage_sessions, triage_snoozes, tasks, briefings, plus existing intelligence_executions extended, plus existing vault_items repurposed); 280+ new backend tests; 50+ Playwright specs; 13 Intelligence prompts seeded; ~25 API route modules added; ~8 shared frontend components.

**Docs**: See `UI_UX_ARC.md` at project root for full arc reference + post-arc backlog + September Wilbert demo script.

#### Vertical-Aware User-Facing Text

Any user-facing example, placeholder, or entity-specific language in the arc UI **must** adapt to the current tenant's vertical via `useVerticalExample(category)` (or `getVerticalExample(vertical, category)` for non-React callers). Hardcoded examples like `"new case"` or `"new order"` are a platform bug — they break trust for tenants in other verticals who immediately register the platform doesn't know what business they're in.

The hook (`frontend/src/hooks/useVerticalExample.ts`) is the single source of truth. 8 categories × 4 verticals:

| category | manufacturing | funeral_home | cemetery | crematory |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `primary_entity` | order | case | burial | cremation |
| `primary_entity_plural` | orders | cases | burials | cremations |
| `primary_detail_term` | order details | case file | burial record | cremation record |
| `secondary_entity` | quote | service | plot | service |
| `new_primary` | new order | new case | new burial | new cremation |
| `new_secondary` | new quote | new service | new plot | new service |
| `workflow_verb` | process | arrange | coordinate | schedule |
| `queue_primary` | invoice | approval | approval | certificate |

Null / unknown verticals fall back to `manufacturing`. Input is case-insensitive and accepts both `funeral_home` and `funeralhome` variants.

**Who must use it:** tooltip bodies, command-bar hints, empty-state messages, keyboard help examples, briefing Intelligence prompts.

**Who doesn't need to:** per-vertical routes (e.g. `fh/pages/DirectionHub.tsx` — FH-only by route), vertical-specific action-registry files (`services/actions/funeral_home.ts` — FH-only by definition), saved view renderer empty states (entity metadata's `display_name` already provides per-entity wording like `"Cases"` / `"Sales Orders"` — no vertical substitution needed).

**Briefing prompts** (`briefing.morning` / `briefing.evening`) receive `vertical` as a Jinja variable and branch on it in a "VERTICAL-APPROPRIATE TERMINOLOGY" block that explicitly tells Claude which terms to use and which to avoid. Verified by `backend/tests/test_briefing_vertical_terminology.py` — asserts the rendered prompt contains correct terminology per vertical and excludes cross-vertical terms.

**Test coverage:** `frontend/src/hooks/useVerticalExample.test.ts` (49 tests — 32 matrix + 6 regression guards + 7 normalization + 4 cross-vertical-leak invariants) + `backend/tests/test_briefing_vertical_terminology.py` (17 tests).

**Prompt-seed behavior** (`scripts/seed_intelligence_phase6.py`): Option A idempotent seeding. Fresh install → v1 active. Exactly 1 version + matching content → no-op. 1 version + differing content → deactivate v1, create v2 active (platform update). Multiple versions exist → skip with warning log (admin customization detected; manual reconciliation via Intelligence admin UI). This preserves admin customizations without separate source-tracking infrastructure.

- **Morning and Evening Briefings — Phase 6 of UI/UX Arc (complete):** AI-generated narrative briefings as workday bookends. Morning orients forward; evening closes backward. Phase 6 is **composition over the primitives** — saved views (Phase 2) provide data, triage queues (Phase 5) provide decision counts, spaces (Phase 3) provide role context, Intelligence synthesizes prose. **Migration `r35_briefings_table`**: new `briefings` table alongside the legacy `employee_briefings` table per the approved coexist-with-legacy strategy. Shape: `id` + `company_id` + `user_id` + `briefing_type` (morning/evening) + `generated_at` + `delivered_at` + `delivery_channels` JSONB + `narrative_text` + `structured_sections` JSONB + `active_space_id/name` + `role_slug` + `generation_context` + metrics (duration_ms, cost_usd, tokens) + `read_at` + `created_at`. Indexes: `ix_briefings_user_type_generated` (user + type + DESC), `ix_briefings_company_generated`, and **partial unique `uq_briefings_user_type_date` on `(user_id, briefing_type, DATE(generated_at AT TIME ZONE 'UTC'))`** — enforces one-per-day per type while allowing morning + evening same day. **Different semantics from `employee_briefings`**: legacy uses `(company_id, user_id, briefing_date)` daily unique (one briefing per user per day total); new table allows morning + evening coexist. Zero collision. `employee_briefings` stays read-only legacy forever. **`backend/app/services/briefings/` package** — 7 modules: `types.py` (Pydantic with `extra="forbid"` — BriefingPreferences + StructuredSections + GeneratedBriefing + BriefingDataContext + MORNING/EVENING_DEFAULT_SECTIONS + DEFAULT_MORNING/EVENING_TIME + BriefingType + BriefingSectionKey + DeliveryChannel literals), `preferences.py` (User.preferences.briefing_preferences namespace + `briefings_seeded_for_roles` idempotency tracker matching Phase 2/3 pattern; `seed_preferences_for_user` translates **legacy `AssistantProfile.disabled_briefing_items` blocklist → Phase 6 `enabled_sections` allowlist** via set subtraction — no data loss, clean forward migration, idempotent per role), `data_sources.py` (**imports legacy context builders verbatim per approved coexist strategy — `_build_funeral_scheduling_context`, `_build_precast_scheduling_context`, `_build_invoicing_ar_context`, `_build_safety_compliance_context`, `_build_executive_context`, `_build_call_summary`, `_build_draft_invoice_context` reused as dependencies; months of customer tuning treated as dependencies not legacy**; also aggregates Phase 5 triage queue_count across every queue visible to the user with seeded 30 sec/item time estimate; Phase 3 active-space lookup from `user.preferences`; VaultItem event_type="event" pull for today + tomorrow; narrative_tone via existing `ai_settings_service`), `generator.py` (fires `briefing.morning` / `briefing.evening` via `intelligence_service.execute` with force_json=True; per-user failures log + continue via try/except; idempotent across re-runs because the unique index rejects duplicates even if the window check races), `__init__.py` (public exports). **`POST /api/v1/briefings/v2/*` API** — 7 new endpoints coexisting with the legacy `/briefings/briefing` + `/briefings/action-items` + `/briefings/team-config` paths (route coexistence under the same router per approved spec item #3): `GET /v2` (list most-recent-first), `GET /v2/latest?briefing_type=X` (returns latest or null), `GET /v2/preferences` (calls `seed_preferences_for_user` on first access for the legacy-blocklist → allowlist translation), `PATCH /v2/preferences` (Pydantic-validated;
